[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe AddressSanitizer shadow memory dump shows:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The problematic address [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x502000000080[0m[39m range[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m contains a partially addressable [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte marker [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m07[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes of an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte chunk are accessible[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow attempts to read the 8th byte which is marked as a heap redzone [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfa[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This confirms an off-by-one read error where the code attempts to access one byte[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the allocated buffer[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a holistic understanding of this vulnerability, the following components [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be examined:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Source File**: `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m603[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m55[0m[39m in the `json_parse_ex` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexact overflow location[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Input data handling and preparation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Management**: [0m                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/json.[0m[1;92mc:279[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m281[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m279[0m[39m:      for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr = json ;; ++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m280[0m[39m:      [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m281[0m[39m:         json_char b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate.ptr == end ? [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m : *state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/json.[0m[1;92mc:955[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m959[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m955[0m[39m:json_value * json_parse [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst json_char * json, size_t length[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m956[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m957[0m[39m:   json_settings settings = [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m958[0m[39m:   return json_parse_ex [0m[1;39m([0m[39m&settings, json, length, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m959[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter examining the evaluation report and code snippets, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability and all related instances that need[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto be fixed.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is an off-by-one error in boundary checking when using [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpre-increment operators. The pattern `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` increments `state.ptr` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBEFORE dereferencing it. When the code checks `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < N` and then [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperforms N pre-increment operations, it actually reads at positions `state.ptr+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough `state.ptr+N`, requiring N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m total positions from the current location. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, the check only ensures N positions are available.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Crash Location Analysis[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report shows a crash at line [0m[1;36m603[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m55[0m[39m in `json_parse_ex`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich is parsing the [0m[32m"true"[0m[39m literal. The shadow memory dump confirms a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte buffer, consistent with an off-by-one boundary check error.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### All Vulnerable Locations[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the code analysis and vulnerability specifications, there are [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m instances [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof this pattern in `src/json.c`:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mVulnerability #[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Unicode escape `\uXXXX` - checks `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` but [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperforms [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m pre-increments[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mVulnerability #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m & #[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Unicode surrogate pair - checks `< [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` but [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperforms [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m pre-increments  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCrash location[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: [0m[32m"true"[0m[39m literal - checks `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` but performs [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpre-increments[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mVulnerability #[0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: [0m[32m"false"[0m[39m literal - checks `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` but performs [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpre-increments[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mVulnerability #[0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: [0m[32m"null"[0m[39m literal - checks `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` but performs [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpre-increments[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe parsing logic is part of a widely-used JSON parser library [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjson-parser from [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGitHub[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The fix must:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintain the exact parsing semantics for valid JSON[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Preserve the two-pass parsing strategy[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keep the same error handling paths[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange: if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReason: [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m pre-increment operations require [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m positions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m more[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReason: [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m pre-increment operations require [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m positions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurrent + [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m more[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only modifies the specific boundary check thresholds, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving all parsing logic[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistent Pattern**: All fixes follow the same principle - increment the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck value by [0m[1;36m1[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Reference Patches**: Matches the good patches provided in the vulnerability [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifications[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: These are purely defensive boundary checks that reject [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid input earlier[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Comprehensive**: Addresses all [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m vulnerable locations in a single fix[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All valid JSON inputs that previously parsed correctly will continue to parse [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The only behavioral change is that truncated inputs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthat would have crashed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m now[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfail gracefully with an error[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The two-pass parsing strategy remains intact[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Error messages and line/column tracking are unaffected[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory allocation patterns are unchanged[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe crash occurs because when parsing a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte input ending with [0m[32m"t"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor [0m[32m"true"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe check `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` passes [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m ≥ [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but the three pre-increment [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations attempt to read bytes at positions +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, +[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, and +[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. If we're at the [0m[32m't'[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes remaining, the third pre-increment reads position +[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m which is at or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte boundary.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy changing the check to `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`, we ensure there are at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m positions available [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcurrent + [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m more[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before performing the [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m pre-increment operations, preventing any[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds reads.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected** - The changes make the boundary checks more conservative:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Previously accepted truncated inputs that would have crashed now return parse [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merrors[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All valid JSON that parsed successfully will continue to parse successfully[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fixes align with the correct boundary checking pattern already used elsewhere[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the code [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., line [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m for comment handling[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already demonstrates correct boundary checking at line [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb == [0m[32m'*'[0m[39m && state.ptr < [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && state.ptr [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m'/'[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis checks `state.ptr < [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before accessing `state.ptr[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequivalent to checking `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >= [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m`. Our [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfixes apply the same principle to the pre-increment scenarios.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
